TITLE      Evaluation of neutron induced cross sections for P-31  V001600100003 
            by means of statistical model and coupled channel     V001600100004 
            optical model calculations                            V001600100005 
AUTHOR     (B.Strohmaier, M.Uhl)                                  V001600100006 
INSTITUTE  (2AUSIRK)                                              V001600100007 
REFERENCE  (C,78HARWELL,,1184,197809)                             V001600100008 
            Summary,some graphs given                             V001600100009 
           (W,STROHMAIER,19800114)                                V001600100010 
            Numerical data + explanations                         V001600100011 
METHOD     Evaluation                                             V001600100012 
ANALYSIS   Coupled channel optical model (CCOM) and statistical   V001600100013 
            model (SM) calculations for neutron-induced cross     V001600100014 
            sections on P-31 were done, fitting the available     V001600100015 
            experimental data with a single set of parameters.    V001600100016 
           The same optical model parameters were used for the    V001600100017 
            CCOM calculations and for the transmission            V001600100018 
            coefficients for the SM calculations. The other SM    V001600100019 
            parameters were chosen consistently for all described V001600100020 
            reactions.                                            V001600100021 
           Computer code used: IUPITOR1 for CCOM, STAPRE for SM   V001600100022 
            (including preequilibrium decay in the first step)    V001600100023 
           The experimental data used for the fits are given      V001600100024 
            below under REL-REF.                                  V001600100025
